# VGG16 Image Classification
VGG16 Image Classification using TensorFlow Serving and Docker container.

## Setup
1. [Train and Export](#train-and-export)
2. [Run ModelServer Container](#run-modelserver-container)
3. [Call Prediction](#call-prediction)

### Train and Export
1. Train and export the model to be served by TensorFlow using following command:
```
$ python vgg16_export-model.py
```
2. We should see something like this:
```
Using TensorFlow backend.
Start the training...
2019-02-18 10:20:30.301501: W tensorflow/core/platform/cpu_feature_guard.cc:45] The TensorFlow library wasn't compiled to use SSE4.1 instructions, but these are available on your machine and could speed up CPU computations.

Exporting trained model to:  b'./vgg16/1'

### Run ModelServer Container
1. Run ModelServer container using following command:
```
$ docker run -p 8500:8500 \
--name vgg16_tf-serving-model \
--mount type=bind,source=/Users/your_computer_name/vgg16/vgg16,target=/models/vgg16 \
-e MODEL_NAME=vgg16 \
-e EXPOSE_PORT_GRPC=8500 \
-e EXPOSE_PORT_REST=8501 \
-t tensorflow/serving &
```
2. We should see something like this:
```
vgg16 suprapto$ 2019-02-18 03:34:02.432105: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server.cc:82] Building single TensorFlow model file config:  model_name: vgg16 model_base_path: /models/vgg16
2019-02-18 03:34:02.435365: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server_core.cc:461] Adding/updating models.
2019-02-18 03:34:02.435459: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server_core.cc:558]  (Re-)adding model: vgg16
2019-02-18 03:34:02.563079: I tensorflow_serving/core/basic_manager.cc:739] Successfully reserved resources to load servable {name: vgg16 version: 1}
2019-02-18 03:34:02.563163: I tensorflow_serving/core/loader_harness.cc:66] Approving load for servable version {name: vgg16 version: 1}
2019-02-18 03:34:02.563194: I tensorflow_serving/core/loader_harness.cc:74] Loading servable version {name: vgg16 version: 1}
2019-02-18 03:34:02.563791: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/contrib/session_bundle/bundle_shim.cc:363] Attempting to load native SavedModelBundle in bundle-shim from: /models/vgg16/1
2019-02-18 03:34:02.563868: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/reader.cc:31] Reading SavedModel from: /models/vgg16/1
2019-02-18 03:34:02.580107: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/reader.cc:54] Reading meta graph with tags { serve }
2019-02-18 03:34:02.591890: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/platform/cpu_feature_guard.cc:141] Your CPU supports instructions that this TensorFlow binary was not compiled to use: AVX2 FMA
2019-02-18 03:34:02.640218: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/loader.cc:162] Restoring SavedModel bundle.
2019-02-18 03:34:02.968662: W external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/framework/allocator.cc:122] Allocation of 67108864 exceeds 10% of system memory.
2019-02-18 03:34:03.708798: W external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/framework/allocator.cc:122] Allocation of 67108864 exceeds 10% of system memory.
2019-02-18 03:34:04.042248: W external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/framework/allocator.cc:122] Allocation of 411041792 exceeds 10% of system memory.
2019-02-18 03:34:07.150760: W external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/framework/allocator.cc:122] Allocation of 411041792 exceeds 10% of system memory.
2019-02-18 03:34:07.611571: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/loader.cc:138] Running MainOp with key legacy_init_op on SavedModel bundle.
2019-02-18 03:34:07.611673: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/loader.cc:259] SavedModel load for tags { serve }; Status: success. Took 5047784 microseconds.
2019-02-18 03:34:07.613107: I tensorflow_serving/servables/tensorflow/saved_model_warmup.cc:83] No warmup data file found at /models/vgg16/1/assets.extra/tf_serving_warmup_requests
2019-02-18 03:34:07.632821: I tensorflow_serving/core/loader_harness.cc:86] Successfully loaded servable version {name: vgg16 version: 1}
2019-02-18 03:34:07.640491: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server.cc:286] Running gRPC ModelServer at 0.0.0.0:8500 ...
[warn] getaddrinfo: address family for nodename not supported
2019-02-18 03:34:07.646909: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server.cc:302] Exporting HTTP/REST API at:localhost:8501 ...
[evhttp_server.cc : 237] RAW: Entering the event loop ...
```
3. Check the Docker container using following command:
```
$ docker ps -a
```
4. We should see something like this:
```
CONTAINER ID        IMAGE                COMMAND                  CREATED              STATUS              PORTS                              NAMES
a10edf598f3a        tensorflow/serving   "/usr/bin/tf_serving…"   About a minute ago   Up About a minute   0.0.0.0:8500->8500/tcp, 8501/tcp   vgg16_tf-serving-model
```

### Call Prediction
1. Now we can call our model that is running in the Docker container using following command:
```
$ python vgg16_predict.py --image=./bird.jpg
```
2. We should see something like this:
```
Using TensorFlow backend.
The server hostport is:  localhost:8500
The image is:  ./bird.jpg
The result is:  [[('n01592084', 'chickadee', 0.9999990463256836), ('n01560419', 'bulbul', 4.723466417999589e-07), ('n01806567', 'quail', 2.1718486209465482e-07), ('n01580077', 'jay', 1.342526161351998e-07), ('n01601694', 'water_ouzel', 4.206732739930885e-08)]]
Time elapsed: 2.161118984222412
```

## Setup using Bottleneck Features
1. [Train and Export with Bottleneck Features](#train-and-export-with-bottleneck-features)
2. [Run ModelServer Container with Bottleneck Features](#run-modelserver-container-with-bottleneck-features)
3. [Call Prediction with Bottleneck Features](#call-prediction-with-bottleneck-features)

### Train and Export with Bottleneck Features
1. Train and export the model with Bottleneck Features to be served by TensorFlow using following command:
```
$ python vgg16_export-model_bottleneck-features.py
```
2. We should see something like this:
```
Using TensorFlow backend.
Start the training...

### Run ModelServer Container with Bottleneck Features
1. Run ModelServer container using following command:
```
$ docker run -p 8500:8500 \
--name vgg16_bottleneck-features \
--mount type=bind,source=/Users/your_computer_name/vgg16/vgg16_bottleneck-features,target=/models/vgg16_bottleneck-features \
-e MODEL_NAME=vgg16_bottleneck-features \
-e EXPOSE_PORT_GRPC=8500 \
-e EXPOSE_PORT_REST=8501 \
-t tensorflow/serving &
```
2. We should see something like this:
```
2019-02-18 03:46:16.801948: I tensorflow_serving/model_servers/server.cc:82] Building single TensorFlow model file config:  model_name: vgg16_bottleneck-features model_base_path: /models/vgg16_bottleneck-features

2019-02-18 03:46:16.936774: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/platform/cpu_feature_guard.cc:141] Your CPU supports instructions that this TensorFlow binary was not compiled to use: AVX2 FMA
2019-02-18 03:46:16.968424: I external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/cc/saved_model/loader.cc:162] Restoring SavedModel bundle.
2019-02-18 03:46:17.899992: W external/org_tensorflow/tensorflow/core/framework/allocator.cc:122] Allocation of 411041792 exceeds 10% of system memory.

3. Check the Docker container using following command:
```
$ docker ps -a
```
4. We should see something like this:
```
CONTAINER ID        IMAGE                COMMAND                  CREATED             STATUS              PORTS                              NAMES
b63b63ac305b        tensorflow/serving   "/usr/bin/tf_serving…"   36 seconds ago      Up 34 seconds       0.0.0.0:8500->8500/tcp, 8501/tcp   vgg16_bottleneck-features
```

### Call Prediction with Bottleneck Features
1. Now we can call our model that is running in the Docker container using following command:
```
$ python vgg16_predict_bottleneck-features.py --image=./bird.jpg
```

```
